\ifproblemToFind% If it has a desirable problem search the file.
%%\tagged{Ans@ShortAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Integral, Sub@Improper, Func@Exp, File@0068}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0068. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}
Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-8}^\infty{{6 \, x}e^{-4 \, x^{2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-8}^\infty{{6 \, x}e^{-4 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{3}{4} \, e^{\left(-256\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-8}^\infty{{-7 \, x}e^{-x^{2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-8}^\infty{{-7 \, x}e^{-x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{7}{2} \, e^{\left(-64\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\choice{Diverges}

\end{multipleChoice}

\]

\end{problem}

\int_{-7}^\infty{{-9 \, x}e^{-5 \, x^{2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-7}^\infty{{-9 \, x}e^{-5 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{9}{10} \, e^{\left(-245\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{2}^\infty{{8 \, x}e^{-9 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{4}{9} \, e^{\left(-36\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{4}^\infty{{6 \, x}e^{-7 \, x^{2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{4}^\infty{{6 \, x}e^{-7 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{3}{7} \, e^{\left(-112\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\begin{problem}
Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-6}^\infty{{2 \, x}e^{-x^{2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-6}^\infty{{2 \, x}e^{-x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{e^{\left(-36\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0068. \\ \fi

\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-3}^\infty{{4 \, x}e^{-7 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{2}{7} \, e^{\left(-63\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{0}^\infty{{9 \, x}e^{-7 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{9}{14}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0068. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}
Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{3}^\infty{{7 \, x}e^{-3 \, x^{2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0068.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{3}^\infty{{7 \, x}e^{-3 \, x^{2}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{7}{6} \, e^{\left(-27\right)}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}
